(* we can obtain a wfs from an nwfs *)
(* the existence of an algebra map is exactly ||nwfs_R_maps_disp f|| *)
Definition nwfs_R_maps_class {C : category} (n : nwfs C) : morphism_class C :=
    λ (x y : C) (f : x --> y), ∥nwfs_R_maps n f∥.
Definition nwfs_L_maps_class {C : category} (n : nwfs C) : morphism_class C :=
    λ (x y : C) (f : x --> y), ∥nwfs_L_maps n (opp_mor f)∥.


C: category
n: nwfs C
a, b, c, d: C
f: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: C ⟦ c, d ⟧
hf: nwfs_L_maps_class n a b f
hg: nwfs_R_maps_class n c d g
lp f g

              (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
              (nwfs_Σ n f))))

    (* rhs is just pr11 nwfs_Σ n f
        unfold three_mor00; simpl. *)
    
C: category

f: arrow C
pr11 (# (nwfs_L_monad n)
        (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
           (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
              (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
              (nwfs_Σ n f)))) =

        (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
           (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
           (nwfs_Σ n f)))

              (nwfs_Σ n f)))) = ?b

           (nwfs_Σ n f)))

        (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data

           (nwfs_Σ n f))) =

    exact (nwfs_Σ_top_map_id n (mor_to_arrow_ob _)).

arrow_mor11
  (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
     (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
        (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
        (nwfs_Σ n f))
   · δ (nwfs_L_monad n)
       (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
          (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
          (nwfs_Σ n f))) =

  (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
     (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
        (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
        (nwfs_Σ n f))
   · # (nwfs_L_monad n)
       (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
          (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
             (nwfs_L_monad n) (opp_mor (fact_L n f))
             (nwfs_Σ n f))))
 exact (nwfs_Σ_bottom_map_L_is_middle_map_of_Σ _ _).
Qed.

     (f · identity b) f

hl0: f · l = Lf
hl1: l · Rf = identity b
(nwfs_L_maps_class n ^cl) a b f

hl0: f · l = Lf
hl1: l · Rf = identity b
∑ (x' y' : C) (f' : C ⟦ x', y' ⟧),

  (pr1 (fact_L n f))
Rf:= three_mor12 (f,, n f): C ⟦ three_ob1 (f,, n f), b ⟧
l: C ⟦ b, three_ob1 (f,, n f) ⟧
hl0: f · l = Lf
hl1: l · Rf = identity b
nwfs_L_maps_class n (pr11 (fact_L n f))
  (pr21 (fact_L n f)) Lf × retract Lf f

  (internal_paths_rew_r (C ⟦ a, b ⟧)

     (λ p : C ⟦ a, b ⟧, p = Lf · Rf)

l: C ⟦ three_ob1 (f,, n f), a ⟧
hl0: Lf · l = identity a
hl1: l · f = Rf
(nwfs_R_maps_class n ^cl) a b f

C: category
I: hSet
n: nwfs C
a, b: I → C
f: ∏ i : I, C ⟦ a i, b i ⟧
hf: ∏ i : I, nwfs_L_maps n (f i)
CCa: Coproduct I C a
CCb: Coproduct I C b
nwfs_L_maps n (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)


C: category
I: hSet
n: nwfs C

          (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
          (three_mor01
             (pr1 n (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)))
          (identity CCa)
          (CoproductArrow I C CCb
             (λ i : I,
              arrow_mor11 (pr1 (hf i))
              · three_mor11 (# n (ini i))))
          (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof0 C I n a b
             f hf CCa CCb))) =
identity
  (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data (nwfs_L_monad n)
     (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
     (mors_to_arrow_mor
        (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
        (three_mor01
           (pr1 n (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)))
        (identity CCa)
        (CoproductArrow I C CCb
           (λ i : I,
            arrow_mor11 (pr1 (hf i))
            · three_mor11 (# n (ini i))))
        (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof0 C I n a b f
           hf CCa CCb)))

                  (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
                  (three_mor01
                     (pr1 n
                        (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb
                           f))) (identity CCa)
                  (CoproductArrow I C CCb
                     (λ i : I,
                      arrow_mor11 (pr1 (hf i))
                      · three_mor11 (# n (ini i))))
                  (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof0 C
                     I n a b f hf CCa CCb)))))

                      (pr1 n

arrow C ⟦ f i, CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f ⟧
i: I
arrow_mor11
  (pr1 (# n (ini i))
   · pr1
       (# (pr1 n)
          (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
             (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
                (nwfs_L_monad n)
                (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
                (mors_to_arrow_mor
                   (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
                   (three_mor01
                      (pr1 n
                        (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb
                        f))) 
                   (identity CCa)
                   (CoproductArrow I C CCb
                      (λ 
                       i : I,
                       arrow_mor11 (pr1 (hf i))
                       · 
                       three_mor11 (# n (ini i))))
                   (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof0 C
                      I n a b f hf CCa CCb)))))) = 
?b
C: category
I: hSet
n: nwfs C
a, b: I → C
f: ∏ i : I, C ⟦ a i, b i ⟧
hf: ∏ i : I, nwfs_L_maps n (f i)
CCa: Coproduct I C a
CCb: Coproduct I C b
ini:= λ i : I,
mors_to_arrow_mor (f i)
  (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
  (CoproductIn I C CCa i) 
  (CoproductIn I C CCb i)
  (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof C I a b f CCa
     CCb i): ∏ i : I,
arrow C ⟦ f i, CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f ⟧
i: I
?b =
arrow_mor11
  (pr1
     (# (pr1 n)
        (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
           (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
              (nwfs_L_monad n) 
              (f i) (pr1 (hf i)))))
   · pr1 (# (pr1 n) (# (fact_L (pr1 n)) (ini i))))
 
C: category
I: hSet
n: nwfs C
a, b: I → C
f: ∏ i : I, C ⟦ a i, b i ⟧
hf: ∏ i : I, nwfs_L_maps n (f i)
CCa: Coproduct I C a
CCb: Coproduct I C b
ini:= λ i : I,
mors_to_arrow_mor (f i)
  (CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f)
  (CoproductIn I C CCa i) 
  (CoproductIn I C CCb i)
  (nwfs_closed_coproducts_subproof C I a b f CCa
     CCb i): ∏ i : I,
arrow C ⟦ f i, CoproductOfArrows I C CCa CCb f ⟧
i: I
arrow_mor11 (pr1 (hf i)) · three_mor11 (# n (ini i)) =
arrow_mor11
  (pr1
     (# (pr1 n)
        (Coalg_map (nwfs_L_monad n)
           (MonadAlgebras.make_Coalgebra_data
              (nwfs_L_monad n) 
              (f i) (pr1 (hf i)))))
   · pr1 (# (pr1 n) (# (fact_L (pr1 n)) (ini i))))

           reflexivity.
Qed.

Definition chain_L_map {C : category}
    (d : chain C) (n : nwfs C) :=
  ∏ (u v : vertex nat_graph) (e : edge u v), nwfs_L_maps n (dmor d e).

Local Definition nwfs_tfcomp_ind_lp
    {C : category}
    {d : chain C}
    (n : nwfs C)
    (CC : ColimCocone d)
    (v : vertex nat_graph) :=
  ∑ (lp : dmor d (idpath (S v)) --> fact_R n (colimIn CC 0)),
    arrow_mor11 lp = colimIn CC (S v).
